[গাজী আজমল স্যার: সংস্করণ-২০২৩, পৃষ্ঠা-৪৯০]</p>

padding-left: 0.289em;">=</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-551" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">s</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-552" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">i</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-553" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">n</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-554" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">90</span><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-555"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-556"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-557" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">°</span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-558" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">⇒</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-559" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">2</span><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-560"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-561"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-562" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">θ</span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-563" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">=</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-564" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">90</span><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-565"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-566"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-567" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">°</span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-568" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">⇒</span><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-569" style="padding-left: 0.289em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-570"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-571" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">θ</span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-572" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">=</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-573" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">45</span><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-574"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-575"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-576" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">°</span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.01em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.098em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.002em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mo stretchy="false">⇒</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">s</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">i</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">n</mi><mn>2</mn><mi>θ</mi><mo>=</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">s</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">i</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">n</mi><mn>90</mn><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><mo>°</mo></mrow><mo stretchy="false">⇒</mo><mn>2</mn><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><mo>θ</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><mn>90</mn><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><mo>°</mo></mrow><mo stretchy="false">⇒</mo><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><mo>θ</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><mn>45</mn><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><mo>°</mo></mrow></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-51">\rm \Rightarrow sin2\theta=sin90°⇒2θ=90°⇒θ=45°</script></span><br>
[ইসহাক স্যার: সংস্করণ-২০২৩, পৃষ্ঠা-১৯৯]</p>
</span>

                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>Complex বাক্যে দুটি clause থাকে যাদের মধ্যে একটি principal clause এবং আরেকটি subordinate clause । সুতরাং প্রদত্ত বাক্যটির complex রূপ হলো As soon as he saw the girl, he fell in love with her।</p>
